The Current Stage of the Sino-Soviet Outstanding Issues 46

Special Article by Hualian News Agency – Since the September 18th Incident, Sino-Soviet relations have become strained. Although the Soviet Union has strongly advocated a policy of peace and made concessions in everything, preventing the tense situation from escalating into war, it is difficult to predict how its future development will be because the Japanese side's attitude is aggressive and unrelenting. The Japanese side's constant pressure on the Soviet Union is using the so-called outstanding issues as a pretext to cover up its military aggression. These outstanding issues include the border issue, the fishery issue, and the oil concession issue. The first issue is the direct cause of the Sino-Soviet conflict. The latter two issues are less important, but they are also "tumors" in the relationship between the two countries, which the Japanese may invoke at any time as a pretext for aggression. The following is an overview of these three outstanding issues for the reference of those concerned about the Sino-Soviet problem.

(1) The North Pacific Fisheries Issue

After the Russo-Japanese War, the Treaty of Portsmouth was signed, and the Japanese obtained fishing rights in the northern part of Sakhalin Island. After the success of the October Revolution, Japan took advantage of the encirclement of the Soviet Union by various imperialist powers, forcibly occupied northern Sakhalin Island, and seized the island's fishing rights. After several twists and turns, because Japan has great ambitions for this, the disputes are not resolved by these two treaties. At present, Japan is only engaged in the fishing industry in the North Pacific, including the fishing areas operated within the Soviet Union's territory under the Japan-Soviet Fisheries Treaty, with an annual output value of more than 40 million yuan, the mother ship-type fishing industry near the Soviet Union's territorial waters, with an annual output value of 10 million yuan, and the drift net fishing industry in the northern Kuril Islands, with an annual output value of 12 million yuan. The treaty concluded in 1928 expired on May 27 this year. According to Article 15 of the treaty, if the parties want to amend the treaty, they should notify the other party twelve months in advance to conduct negotiations. Therefore, Japan proposed three principles to the Soviet Union last year, namely, stabilizing the fishing area for a long-term extension, abolishing the auction system, and stabilizing the ruble, and at the same time requested four additional conditions: (1) fish protection, (2) rectification of the terms of mutual lending fees, (3) prohibition of river fishing issues, (4) fish weight calculation methods, etc., and other details. However, after several negotiations, there have been no results, and it will completely fall into a state of no treaty. Various disputes will inevitably arise in the future.

(2) The Oil Concession Issue

As mentioned earlier, Japan took advantage of the victory in the Russo-Japanese War in 1905, signed the Treaty of Portsmouth, and seized sovereignty over the southern half of Sakhalin Island. In 1922, it took advantage of the success of the October Revolution and the internal order that had not yet been fully restored to occupy the island. It was not until 1925 that it was returned, which shows the ambitions it harbored for the island. The reason why Japan coveted the island is that the island is a producer of forests, oil, and fisheries, and the oil reserves are equal to the amount of gold deposits in Japan. Japan obtained the oil exploration rights on the island in January 1929. Subsequently, the Japan-Soviet Treaty was signed, stipulating that Japan has the right to 50% of the area for oil field exploration on the island, and the remaining 50% gives Japan priority when the Soviet Union allows foreigners to exploit it. Japanese people are also allowed to select 1,000 Russian acres of oil mines on the east coast within ten years and carry out test mining. If the results are excellent, half of the area will be returned to the Japanese for exploration. The validity period of the treaty on Japanese rights and interests in Sakhalin Island is ten years, which expires in December this year. Japan is a country that is congenitally lacking and actively engaged in preparing for war. There is no reason to abandon this kind of national defense resource in the country that is a source of heavy revenue for the country. This is why the air of buying Sakhalin Island in Japan is very high. However, the Soviet Union only allowed the term of the original treaty to be extended to 1938. Now the president of the North Sakhalin Petroleum Corporation, Sakonji, has been traveling between Moscow, Tokyo, and Sakhalin, actively planning to expand operations.

(3) The Border Issue

This issue is deliberately used by Japan as a pretext to create a smokescreen for its aggression. It includes both Manchuria and Mongolia and the Manchuria-Soviet Union border. The Japanese army has repeatedly clashed with the Soviet-Mongolian Red Army under the pretext of the unclear demarcation of this boundary line. According to calculations, from last year to February this year, there were more than 250 such conflict incidents on the "Manchuria"-Soviet Union and "Manchuria"-Mongolia borders. Among these incidents, such as the Jinzhanggou Incident and the Changlingzi Incident, were battles that lasted a day and a night, almost triggering a formal war between Japan and the Soviet Union. Because Japan wants to use this to carry out its huge military plan, divert international attention, and prepare to plunder Siberia, even if it holds meetings with the Soviet and Mongolian delegates, it will eventually refuse peace proposals with excuses. In order to protect their own rights and interests, the Soviet and Mongolian sides have no choice but to redeploy garrison troops in case of emergency. Therefore, there is a danger that the future will develop into a Russo-Japanese War.

Britain Actively Strengthening Defenses in the Far East; Japan Watching its Progress 47

(Tokyo) – Recently, while the British government has been carrying out peace work on the European continent, it has also been focusing on strengthening the regular army and expanding defensive facilities in Hong Kong and Singapore, as a countermeasure when the Washington and London Naval Treaties and the Pacific Fortification Restriction Agreement expire. Because it is quite obvious, the Japanese authorities concerned are watching its progress. Since Japan withdrew from the London Naval Conference, the era of no treaties will appear from 1937 onwards. The British government has established a policy of expanding and strengthening the facilities of its Far East bases, and gradually replacing the ordinary China Fleet with new warships, and is gradually implementing it. In particular, the fortification work in Singapore has made obvious progress. Most of the expansion of shipyards and the expansion of fortresses will be completed and prepared by the end of this year. The permanent garrison force in Singapore will also be strengthened to three times the current army force of 30,000 people, and the air force force is also being expanded. In Hong Kong, a plan has been established to complete modern mechanical troops. The air force is also expanding the current aircraft and is planning to implement the construction of a new airfield. (Allied dispatch, 26th)

Conditions for Italy and Germany to Participate in Future Five-Power Conference; Britain Prepares to Announce Revocation of Mediterranean Mutual Assistance Agreement 48

(London) – Italy and Germany have been formally invited to participate in the future five-power conference, but it is still uncertain whether they will accept. Regarding this matter, "The Observer" recently reported that German leader Hitler and Italian Prime Minister Mussolini used long-distance telephones to discuss with each other. It is heard that both of them will put forward conditions for participating in the conference. What Hitler requested is that all countries should allow Germany to develop in Africa. Mussolini advocated that the mutual assistance agreements signed by the Mediterranean countries should be revoked first. As for the latter, "The Sunday Times" reported that when Foreign Secretary Eden attends the House of Commons tomorrow, he will announce that he will revoke it. (Havas dispatch, 26th)

(Rome) – Britain, France, and Belgium have formally invited Italy to participate in the future five-power conference. Italy's reply has not yet been sent. Regarding this matter, responsible persons recently stated that Italy will definitely insist that all kinds of measures similar to sanctions adopted by various countries must be abolished, and Italy can cooperate again on European events. As for Italy's conquest of Abyssinia, the government does not intend to ask other countries to recognize it. It has never made this request before, and has only notified the powers of the fait accompli. (Havas dispatch, 25th)

(London) – Well-informed sources recently declared that Italy and Germany will definitely accept to participate in the future five-power conference. It is heard that German officials are very pleased with this. (1) The British Home Fleet has withdrawn from the Mediterranean and returned to its original defense. The British naval power there has been reduced to normal figures. Although several warships of the Home Fleet have repeatedly sailed into the Mediterranean, their purpose is only to transport nationals out of Spain to seek refuge, just like France, the United States, Italy, and Germany have done, with no other purpose. (2) The mutual assistance agreement previously signed by Britain and the Mediterranean countries will be revoked soon. The reason why the agreement has been maintained to this day is nothing more than the following two points: (A) Internal political reasons, (B) Negotiations between Britain and Egypt are still in progress, so it is not convenient to allow Italy to act freely in the Mediterranean. Now that the British-Egyptian negotiations are almost completely completed, the government will explain the suspicions of the talks between Britain, France, and Belgium in the House of Commons, and it is hoped that a lasting solution can be found for the European situation. At the same time, it will announce the cancellation of the Mediterranean Mutual Assistance Agreement. The date is probably next Monday (28th). According to predictions in the political circles, before Germany and Italy are sure to accept to participate in the Five-Power Conference, they will ask Britain to explain the purpose of the meeting. Therefore, the three countries still need to conduct long-term negotiations through diplomatic channels. (Havas dispatch, 25th)

European Crisis Lurking; Formation of Confrontational Groups Forming a Pre-War Situation; Saving War Depends on Cooperation of All Countries – Speech by Sir Simon of Britain – 49

West Sussex, Canterbury, Britain – Home Secretary Simon recently delivered a speech here, elaborating on the situation in Europe, stating that the people of the three signatory countries of the Locarno Treaty (i.e., Britain, France, and Belgium) should pay attention to the light talk held in London on the 23rd of this month. However, the facts show that the people mostly ignore it, which is really abnormal. We must know that there is a great danger in Europe today. What is it? That is, the European countries have formed several groups through alliances, confronting each other and preparing for war. This situation is bad and old, and it was actually seen before 1914, which eventually led to the outbreak of the European War. Why is it being replayed now? The crisis is lurking, needless to say. The policy pursued by our government has always been aimed at reversing this situation and bringing the European countries together in one room to discuss common problems in a free and friendly manner. The reason is that common problems can only be solved by the joint cooperation and concerted efforts of all parties. A month ago, this kind of cooperation seemed quite dim, but today it has suddenly become clear, and the time for its realization is not far away. Britain, France, and Belgium have now stated that they are prepared to cooperate in order to solve all kinds of difficult problems. If Germany and Italy also hold the same view, then the gap between each other can be bridged. Do Germany and Italy also have intentions in this regard? This is what we earnestly hope for. Simon then criticized the opposition Labor Party for opposing the supplementary defense budget proposal, and criticized the pessimists who thought that war was inevitable, saying that there are people whispering privately that war is inevitable. This kind of argument is mediocre and dangerous. I will strongly refute it and hope that the people of the country will jointly close it. After our country's strength has reached its peak, it will not only not cause war, but also be sufficient to guarantee peace. (Havas dispatch, 25th)

Britain and Egypt Sign New Treaty; Military Clauses Initialed 50

Cairo – Regarding the conclusion of a new treaty between Britain and Egypt, the delegations of both sides yesterday initialed an agreement on various military clauses. The main points are as follows: (1) The number of British troops stationed in Egypt shall not exceed 10,000, and their defense area shall be limited to the Suez Canal area. If the Egyptian army is capable of defending the territory after 20 years, then the British troops shall withdraw completely. Regarding this, if there is a dispute between the two countries, it shall be submitted to the League of Nations for arbitration. (2) The airfields built by Britain in Egypt at Abu Qir and Heliopolis shall be abandoned, but two new airfields may be built near Port Suez and Moska to replace them. (3) In peacetime, Britain may not use any Egyptian port as a naval base. If a war occurs, British warships may use these ports, but prior approval from the Egyptian government must be obtained. (4) The Egyptian government may freely increase its troop strength without seeking British consent. (Havas dispatch, 26th)

German Minister to Austria, Papen, Promoted to Ambassador; German Agreements Progressively Implemented; Freedom Restored to National Socialist Party Members 51

(Berlin) German Minister to Austria, Papen, was promoted to Ambassador Extraordinary and Plenipotentiary to Austria by Führer Hitler in recognition of his contributions to the German-Austrian Agreement signed on July 11. However, the diplomatic representation of Germany in Vienna will remain at the level of a legation as before. (National Telegram, 25th)

Vimy Memorial Inaugurated in France to Commemorate Fallen Canadian Soldiers; British King Presides Over Ceremony 54

Vimy, France: The Canadian War Memorial built on the hillside here to commemorate Canadian soldiers who died in the European War will be officially inaugurated this afternoon by King Edward VIII of England and French President Lebrun. At the time, there will be 6,000 Canadian veterans, 600 officials from Britain, France, and Canada, and over 100,000 people in attendance. King Edward VIII departed from Portsmouth harbor last night aboard the Royal Yacht and is scheduled to arrive at 2:00 PM today. The inauguration ceremony is scheduled to begin with a brief religious service. Canadian Prime Minister Mackenzie King will then deliver a congratulatory speech from Canada via long-distance telephone. The British King and the French President will then unveil the memorial and deliver speeches. At that time, several British and French military aircraft will fly over the memorial several times. The inauguration ceremony will then be completed. The memorial is based on stone, extending 320 feet, symbolizing the wartime defensive line. Stone pillars, each 150 feet high, stand on both sides. The pillars are surrounded by sculptures by renowned Canadian sculptor Allward, symbolizing Canadian soldiers and their ideals. Construction took ten years and cost 15 million francs. It can be described as a great project. (Havas News Agency, 26th)

Reply Regarding Receipt of Funds; Stamp Duty Should be Affixed if No Receipt is Issued 60

(Nanjing) The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce inquired of the Ministry of Finance whether a reply regarding the receipt of funds should have stamp duty affixed. The Ministry of Finance replied that the reply regarding the receipt of funds is the same as a cash receipt and can be used as a substitute voucher. Stamp duty should be affixed. If a receipt was issued upon receiving the funds, stamp duty does not need to be affixed. However, if discovered by inspectors, the name, address, amount, and date of receipt must be verified as identical. Also the receipt with sufficient stamp duty should be presented for proof, otherwise, it will be treated as a failure to affix stamp duty and a fine will be imposed. (Special Dispatch, 26th)

Zou and Song Arrive in Guangdong to Reorganize Finance; Zou Lin to First Return to Nanjing After Investigating the Situation; Song Ziliang Has Already Assumed the Post of Acting Director of the Finance Department; Guangdong's Foreign Exchange Declines, Central Government Bonds Rise 83

Guangzhou Correspondence: In this political change in Guangdong, the former Director of the Finance Department, Ou Fangpu, has been dismissed along with Chen Jitang. Merchants and businessmen believe that the Guangdong affair has been settled, and the wholesale and retail of goods have returned to normal. The financial community is not as prone to manipulating Hong Kong exchange rates as it was a few days ago, so the value of the Hong Kong dollar has fallen from a premium of nine to a premium of six or seven. The newly appointed Director of the Finance Department, Song Ziliang, arrived in Guangzhou by plane at 3:00 PM on the 22nd. Accompanying him were Zou Lin, a financial decision maker; Zhou Shouliang, deputy director of the Business Department of the Central Bank; Hao Chongguang of the Central Trust Bureau; financial experts Tang Shi and Dong Rending; and Wu Jiantao, the newly appointed Director of the Guangdong-Guangxi-Fujian Unified Tax Bureau, totaling eleven people. When the Nanjing aircraft carrying Song, Zou, and others flew south, it flew over Shaoguan and landed in Shao to first meet with Yu Hanmou to discuss in detail the measures for reorganizing the finances of Guangdong Province. After three or four minutes, he took the original aircraft to Guangdong, and after getting off the aircraft, took a car to the city guesthouse to rest. Welcomers were immediately there where a tea party was held. Fan Zhanpeng of the Anti-Smuggling Office gave a welcome speech, and Zou Lin replied, saying that he was ordered by the Ministry of Finance to come to Guangdong to inspect the progress of Guangdong's financial reorganization. Then Song Ziliang gave a speech and dispersed. In the evening, Provincial Chairman Lin Yunhao hosted a banquet. On this day, Zou and Song made the following remarks: "Guangdong is the source of the revolution, and it is also an important coastal port. The development of foreign trade has a considerable position in the international arena. Therefore, the central government attaches more importance to Guangdong than any other place. For several years, there has been no opportunity to seek a complete reorganization. The government authorities have been distressed. Now that the Guangdong situation has been settled and the obstacles have been eliminated, everyone knows that there is no way to save the country and survive without unified political orders. This is the government's long-standing desire to seek welfare and cooperation for the people of Guangdong. It can be expected to be implemented. Finance and finance are the lifeline, and reorganization cannot be delayed. Minister Kong specially dispatched Lin as a representative to Guangdong to inspect, and at the same time, he accepted the decision of the Executive Yuan to appoint Ziliang as a special financial commissioner of Guangdong and concurrently as the director of the Finance Department. We originally planned to come by sea, but Minister Kong believed that the reputation bureau had just been settled, and the people's hearts were uneasy. It is not possible to make important officials Lu Xuan and important political affairs stalled. I hope that the arrangement in Guangdong will be properly settled, and my heart is extremely urgent, so I changed to a plane. When I first arrived in Guangdong, I should formulate an entire plan on how to organize the entire finance and finance. After a thorough investigation of the details, I will prepare a plan and submit it to the central or local government for approval and implementation, step by step. I hope that it will be beneficial to both the national economy and the people's livelihood, and that it will not disappoint the expectations of the people of Guangdong." On the 23rd, Song had already assumed the post of Guangdong Financial Commissioner and concurrently acting Director of the Guangdong Finance Department. Zou Lin will first return to Beijing to report to Minister Kong after inspecting the financial situation in Guangdong Province and investigating finance. Also, Tang Haian took over as acting Salt Transport Commissioner on the afternoon of the 21st. During the day, he will find ways to reorganize salt affairs and save the past decline. Since Zou and Song arrived in the province, they have claimed to reorganize Guangdong's finances, so the general merchants and people deeply hope that the government bonds issued by the Central Government in Guangdong in the past will be reorganized. In recent days, the prices of the first and second phases of the Central Government bonds have risen to 37, the third phase of the Central Government bonds has risen to 34, and the National Defense bonds have risen to 30%. The ten-yuan central banknotes issued by the Central Bank in Guangdong suddenly rose from 40% to 70%. The financial market is very active in trading such bonds. (July 23rd)

Songjiang: Black Fever Discovered in This City 86

He Runzhang, Director of the Public Security Bureau, believes that beggars begging in the city are a nuisance to the city's appearance, and that the number of beggars coming from outside has been increasing recently. Therefore, he and local figures and Zhou Xuewen, director of the Red Cross Society, negotiated to organize a beggar shelter in the Gushui Daoyuan. More than 40 male and female beggars have been captured, provided with meals, and taught skills so that they can support themselves. Yesterday, a male beggar named Wang Guirong, 17 years old, from Jiangbei, was diagnosed with fever, also known as ganglioma, which is quite serious. Director He believes that black fever is now prevalent in the Huai, Xu, and Hai areas and spreads quickly. It has not yet been discovered in this city. In order to avoid its spread, he has sent the sick beggar to the Shanghai Municipal Hospital for treatment to avoid future troubles.

Common Malpractice: Accumulation of Problems in the Land Tax Collection Office 87

The land tax in this county has always been collected by the East and West Land Tax Collection Offices of the county government. The heads of the two offices are both local residents, and because the collection procedures are complicated, experienced personnel are required, which has become a hereditary practice. Therefore, even with frequent changes of county magistrates, the heads of the two offices have never been replaced, leading to the proliferation of malpractices. Now, after assuming office, the county magistrate, in order to thoroughly rectify the situation, has specially recruited more than fifty accountants, and starting from the 15th of this month, they have begun to investigate the accumulated records of the two offices over the years. It is said that many malpractices have been discovered. For example, due to the preservation of collection records being incomplete and unclear regarding whether property owners have fully paid their debts, for a considerable portion of wealthy households, internal staff members undertake to handle the payments. For instance, if a payment of one thousand yuan is due, they first pay three hundred yuan, and the staff member is responsible for it. No receipt is issued, and no further collection is pursued. The funds are pocketed by the staff member, and this malpractice has persisted for a long time without ever being discovered. Currently, the county government will thoroughly rectify the situation, and some people propose that the names of the households with outstanding records should be formally announced to clarify the matter. It is believed that the amount of arrears owed by these officials is tens of times greater than that owed by the common people.

Plea for Postponement of Income Tax Collection 88

Pang Diancai, chairman of the county chamber of commerce, due to the recent sluggish business of various merchants, telegraphed the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Finance, requesting a temporary postponement of income tax collection. The original text was quite lengthy, and the main points raised four reasons: (1) Merchants are already paying business tax, and if they have to pay income tax as well, the combined tax rate would be too high; (2) Various exorbitant taxes such as production and sales donation, bandit suppression and rehabilitation donation, special tax, consumption tax, silk improvement tax, special tax, landing tax, slaughter tax, tobacco and alcohol tax, etc., have not been abolished. If income tax is implemented, these similar "likin" style policies should be completely abolished; (3) From an individual perspective, if a monthly salary is thirty yuan, it is not even enough to support a family, let alone have any surplus; (4) Income tax will inevitably not be extended to foreigners, so in the future, merchants in concessions may not be easily collected from, resulting in domestic savings and public bonds being deposited in foreign banks, promoting the escape of capital, and the hope of revival for industry and commerce will be forever lost.

Jiangyin: Clues Obtained in Homicide Case in the Urban Area 89

Tong Lu's, the wife of Tong Degen, a resident behind Wenheng Bridge in the city, allowed Zhang Goulang, the 62-year-old nephew of Zhang Aliu who lived across the street, to stay in their home, but he was suddenly killed. After investigation by the county government, according to Tong Lu's, three or four days earlier, a person surnamed Jia from another province stated that he was unfavorable to Tong Lu's, and it is speculated that Zhang Goulang's murder might be related to this person. However, there are factual difficulties in this case, and the county government is seeking a way to extradite the person surnamed Jia from another province.

Jinan Railway Bureau: Purchasing the Boshan Light Railway, Purchase Price of 780,000 Already Approved by the Ministry of Railways 90

Jinan dispatch: The Boshan Light Railway is a major privately-operated coal transport route in the Liubo mining area. However, due to the excessively high freight rates and the inability to connect with the Zhangbo branch line of the Jiaoji Railway, the coal industry in eastern Shandong and the transportation revenue of the Jiaoji Railway have both been affected. The Boshan Light Railway, due to poor management, has been heavily indebted. Two years ago, there was already a proposal to sell it to the Jiaoji Railway. The Jiaoji Railway also eagerly wanted to purchase it due to the above-mentioned reasons. However, due to various reasons, the purchase issue was discussed and then discontinued. Recently, after negotiations between the provincial government and the Boshan Light Railway, it was agreed to purchase it for 780,000 yuan. Later, because the Ministry of Railways only agreed to pay 650,000 yuan, which was more than 100,000 yuan less than the original agreement, the issue almost stalled. Tu Wei-zeng, the chief of engineering of the Jiaoji Railway, was sent to Beijing to explain everything to the Ministry of Railways. The board of directors of the Boshan Light Railway convened a meeting of creditor groups in Jinan, submitted a request to the construction department to be forwarded to the provincial government, and informed the Jiaoji Railway that it agreed to sell it for 780,000 yuan. Now, the Ministry of Railways has sent a telegram to the Jiaoji Railway Administration, formally approving the purchase for 780,000 yuan. As for the method of appropriation, the Ministry of Railways will send personnel to Qingdao to handle it. Today (the 23rd), the Jiaoji Railway Administration has forwarded this telegram to Ge Guangting. Tonight (the 23rd), Ge has returned to Qingdao from Jinan. Once the personnel from the Ministry of Railways arrive, the payment can be made and the purchase realized. The issue of purchasing the Boshan Light Railway, which has been brewing for more than two years, has now been successfully concluded. (23rd)

Nantong: Negotiations on Japanese Fishing Boat Intrusion 92

Ge Tan, the special commissioner of the Fourth District of Jiangsu Province, telegraphed the provincial government to promptly consult the Ministry and negotiate with the Japanese side regarding the intrusion of Japanese fishing boats into the Shengsi Islands and the destruction of our fishing industry. The telegram stated briefly: According to a telegraph from Gu Hongxi, the magistrate of Chongming County, on behalf of the district magistrate of the Fifth District, Ling Pengcheng, the case of fishing boats anchored in Sijiao being destroyed by Japanese fishing boats has been reported by the district magistrate in a telegraph, and has been submitted to the Ministry and provincial government for rescue and negotiation. Now, fishermen Wang Ade and others have managed to borrow nets and other equipment and go out to fish again, hoping for a final struggle to make a living. Unexpectedly, they were again destroyed by dozens of unknown Japanese fishing boats and the domestic hand-operated net fishing boats, De Tai No. 1 and No. 2, which completely dragged away 131 tiers of nets from the 16 households. Their livelihood is now completely cut off, and they must also compensate for the borrowed nets, selling everything to make ends meet. They plead to be telegraphed to the upper levels for rescue. It is investigated that the people have previously suffered significant losses, and now they have been devastated again. The district authorities have witnessed the situation and believe that their livelihoods have been cut off. In addition to instructing local wealthy households to provide assistance to temporarily alleviate hunger, it is appropriate to telegraph the request for transfer to the investigation and joint negotiations. As for the domestic fishing boats De Tai No. 1 and No. 2, they are conscienceless and harm their own kind, and it is requested to investigate and prosecute them according to the law. Based on this, it is investigated that the district magistrate previously reported that Japanese fishing boats had crossed the border to intrude and drag away fishing nets, and the case has been reported. According to the telegram, in addition to instructions, it is appropriate to telegraph the request for joint review.

Yangzhou: Jufeng Township Robbed by Bandits 93

The home of Yan Yulou, the head of the ninth bao and sixth jia of Jufeng Township, the seventh district under the county, which is close to Taixian County, was suddenly invaded by many bandits with firearms the other night. They rushed inside, intimidated Yulou, his son Yongxin, and the hired workers, and detained them in a room to rob them. Fortunately, his daughter-in-law, Xie, took the opportunity to climb onto the roof and escape to call for help. The neighbors heard the alarm and started ringing gongs. Yan Ruzhen and Yan Buhai, the heads of the fifth and sixth jia of the bao, were seriously injured while resisting the bandits. Later, the neighboring villages also heard the alarm and burned straw piles and fired shots to show their strength, which frightened the bandits and dispersed them. After the incident, an investigation revealed that the Yan family only lost the bao chief's official seal and some miscellaneous items.

In order to concentrate agricultural products and circulate the rural economy, the Zhejiang Construction Department decided to establish an agricultural warehouse management committee. Ningbo: Sand Boat Hits Reef, Many Killed 95

The Jinxinsheng sand boat, with a very large capacity, was owned by boat owner Ding Zhicheng, who hired 15 crew members including Xu Asheng, Shen Chunsheng, Lu Baocheng, Xu Linsheng, and Lu Dalai. Ding Zhicheng had a concubine, He, and a four-year-old son, Bogao, who resided in Xiamen. On the 21st, the boat carried 1,245 bags of brown sugar from Xiamen, worth more than 30,000 yuan. The cargo owner gave a deadline of five days to transport the sugar to Yongbo. Therefore, after leaving the harbor of Xiamen, the boat sailed day and night without stopping. At about 3:00 PM on the 23rd, the boat sailed through the Yushan waters of the Zhejiang Sea, and suddenly encountered a hidden reef, which broke the hull. Because they only knew that the front cargo hold had been breached, they rushed to repair it, causing the breach in the rear cargo hold to burst open. Sea water poured in and could not be blocked. The boat sank in an instant. At that time, there was a strong wind and rain, and there were no boats on the sea. There was no one to call for help. Only three crew members, Xu Asheng, Shen Chunsheng, and Lu Baocheng, were rescued by a fishing boat after floating in the water for two hours. The remaining 15 people, including Ding Zhicheng, were buried in the belly of the fish. It was a truly tragic disaster. Hu Dingren, the magistrate of Xiangshan County, secretary Zhu Wenbo, the third section chief Guo Yaohou, and gentry Feng Yixin, Kong Xianbin, and Zhang Zaixi, etc., were reported to the Fujian-Zhejiang supervisory commissioner for punishment due to the opium suppression case and the appropriation of artificial silk bonuses for the Damaitang ticket purchase. The commissioner specially dispatched Chen to Xiangshan a few days ago to thoroughly investigate the truth, inquire about the truth from all parties involved and relevant parties, and returned to the province to report after inspecting the case files in the county. (23rd)

Xiaoshan: Four Children Drown While Swimming 96

In Jinjishan near Sheqian in the southern countryside of Xiaoshan, the mountains are green and the water is clear. Every summer, there are many people swimming and bathing all day long. On the morning of the 25th of this month, four children surnamed Li and Fang were learning to swim in a stream in the area. Unexpectedly, because the stream water flowed down from top to bottom, plunging straight down, the children did not know how to swim. They jumped in, went from shallow to deep, and drifted away with the current. It was not until the afternoon that the families looked for the children and went to the area to check. They only saw four sets of clothes. By 4:00 PM, the bodies had not surfaced.

Donghai: Bandits Burn and Loot Huahou Township 97

Since Gaoliang in the county became restless, Xu Guilin, the bandit leader from Guanyun, gathered more than 30 followers and occupied Huahou Township in the first district of Guanyun. The township has the former and latter villages of Xu Shanglin. After the bandits occupied the former village, the latter village learned of it, and Jia Jie led the villagers to besiege the former village on the night of the 18th. The bandits resisted in the village, and the two sides fought fiercely for two hours. The aftermath of the former village is now being handled, and the losses are considerable.

Anecdotes from the Southern Tour: Special Correspondent Shi Ying of This Newspaper - Forced Education in Jiangshan 98

The people of Jiangshan are tough, and the gentry are divided into factions. Every county magistrate who comes here feels a headache. In the past, only two county magistrates earned a good reputation: one was called Chen Dingxin, because he was fair and honest. He knew that the common people could not squeeze water out of dry firewood, so he truly donated his official salary to subsidize the mandatory and miscellaneous items sent down from above. The other was called Wu Yimin, who was bold and courageous. When he encountered difficult theft cases, he dared to disguise himself and capture the robbers. Naturally, this is not enough to call them upright officials of a prosperous age, but what day is it today? What's more, Jiangshan is a place where the people are poor and there are many bandits. It is no wonder that the common people praise and remember these two county magistrates who "do not love money" and "are not afraid of death."

The current county magistrate, Zhou Xinwan, has served for four or five consecutive terms. Of course, he has achieved considerable political achievements. Otherwise, how could he have done it? It is said that Zhou County Magistrate suffered a loss of more than 30,000 yuan in savings when Cuifeng Zhuang in Qu County went bankrupt, and his request for reimbursement from the provincial government was rejected. However, according to the idle talk of several gentry, being a county magistrate also has its hardships.

Later, the reporter went to visit him, and he talked about several valuable political views:

He said: "First, the current county administration is not worried about the lack of plans, but is actually worried about too many plans. Sometimes, the superiors issue too many government orders that they cannot even remember themselves, and then issue new orders that change the method or contradict the previous ones. As a result, what has been done below loses credibility with the people, and what has not been done is lucky to please. There are even government orders that have good motives, but the result is a policy that harms the people. For example, labor service, digging soil and building roads, five amateurish and weak people are often not as good as an experienced laborer. Even if the government does not pay, the people are not all idle class, and going to work is equivalent to spending money. Second, the increase in the duties of the Bao chief also has more disadvantages than advantages. For example, fighting bandits, allocating funds, grain for soldiers, training militia, and soliciting donations for airplanes are five major events that the county government is worried about not being able to do, and are completely pushed on the Bao chief. The mission of a Bao chief has become a microcosm of the county government's authority. As a result, the fault is that there is no movement when there should be movement, or no movement at all. Third, many financial institutions that help the countryside, such as bank loans and cooperative organizations, are not purely launched from an objective perspective, but from a subjective perspective. To be specific, few banks that arrive are not absorbed by it to deposit funds and manipulate market prices. Mr. Chen Lifu once said: 'Banks are the enemy of the countryside.' The financial community, which hopes to use the good name of helping the countryside to achieve profit-making purposes, should deeply reflect on this." This conversation, rich in experienced meaning, is revealed frankly. A virtuous and capable county magistrate should not be offended, right?

The Inter-Provincial Bandit Suppression Headquarters of the four provinces of Zhejiang, Jiangxi, Anhui, and Fujian also stands in this small city, which is also known as "Jade Leaf." The commander-in-chief is Zhang Fakui, the commander of the Fourth Army, known as the "Iron Army" in the Northern Expedition era. During the tense January 28th Shanghai Incident, many people and public opinion longed for this "Iron General" to descend from the sky and show his skills. At this time, mentioning the name Zhang Fakui, readers probably feel somewhat familiar. This time, when the reporter went to visit him, he talked a lot about the national crisis and current affairs in a passionate and excited manner, but he also instructed us not to publish it for the time being. But readers do not need to be disappointed. His secretary, the chief of the secretariat, Wang Kuiyi, and other gentlemen, unintentionally talked about Zhang's interesting stories during his European tour, which is a good alternative dessert:

On the train to Germany, a German with deep eyes and a high nose saw him dressed elegantly and acting dignified, and gave him a thumbs up to congratulate him, saying: "Admire! Admire! Your country's military strength is really strong. It won't be long before you occupy half of China!" Zhang knew that the man had mistaken him for a Japanese and was filled with shame and indignation. But the man still rambled on. Zhang had not yet reached his destination and had to sacrifice his plan and get off the train first. Later, when he arrived in Berlin, he wanted to visit a factory and hired a famous teacher to teach him German at a price of eighty marks per hour. When Zhang filled out the resume form, he did not directly fill in "soldier" but pretended to be a history teacher. Unexpectedly, the teacher looked at the resume during the first class and suddenly asked him as if he had found something: "Japan is constantly invading China. China has six or seven times the population and dozens of times the land of Japan. Why doesn't it resist? Since you are a history teacher, please tell me: What is the Chinese national character?" This is another difficult question that he still cannot forget. Readers, how does this dessert taste?

The headquarters leads the local government to promote local construction, improve customs, and implement compulsory education as much as possible. The South Main Street in the city is lined with shops and is the most prosperous area in the city, but the street is so narrow that it "can be" narrow. Moreover, during labor service, the newly built "strip" and "cattle" roads are often secretly discussed by the common people, saying that they wear out a few more pairs of shoes than the old roads. Every time at dusk, shop assistants set up seats along the street and fan themselves to enjoy the cool air. Not only do passers-by have difficulty passing each other face to face, but the sweaty air that fills the street seems to have nowhere to evaporate. Now the headquarters has ordered the demolition of houses to widen the road and applied to the provincial government for a subsidy of 6,000 yuan (which has been agreed upon but not yet received) to be used for repairing the road surface. Although this matter is inevitably difficult in action, the result can make transportation convenient, improve the city's appearance, and prosper commerce. Therefore, it has begun to be actively carried out, and it is expected that the entire road will be completed after autumn.

Jiangshan is located in a remote corner, and the people mostly adhere to outdated customs, especially when holding funerals, they pay attention to what "Seven Sevens" means. That is, the "First Seven" opens the mourning hall, and relatives and friends come to offer condolences without end. The "Second Seven" makes sacrifices and recites scriptures. The "Third Seven" says that the deceased begins to know that he is dead, and the bereaved family must kneel in the courtyard and cry all night to show filial piety. "Fifth Seven" relatives and friends offer sacrifices and set up a banquet to entertain guests, and prepare for the funeral on the "Seventh Seven" to be considered over. But which year and which direction is auspicious? When will it actually be carried out? These are all problems. According to the investigation, there are as many as three hundred coffins parked in the city, which is a danger to the health of the entire city of more than nine thousand people! Now the headquarters has issued a notice, ordering the funeral to be carried out and stipulating that the mourning period should not exceed "One Seven" in the future. In the past few days when the deadline is approaching, you can almost always hear the sound of trumpets and firecrackers, which are all mourning music to clear out this large number of dead people. However, there are still people who want to change the "One Seven" mourning period to "Three Seven." It is hoped that local people will provide guidance in various ways, because this excessively superstitious and uneconomical and unsanitary funeral should indeed be taken advantage of to improve it once and for all. This is not only the luck of the bereaved family, but also the luck of the local area.

In China at the present stage, implementing compulsory education is often criticized, and it is considered a fantasy and impossible education method. Because China's educational tradition has always adopted a laissez-faire and liberal approach, if it suddenly changes to an interventionist and restrictive approach, then the national situation may present a state of anxiety and uneasiness. At the same time, most of the general public are struggling with hunger and poverty. There is no time to seek knowledge. There are also problems such as teachers and teaching materials, which are strong obstacles in the objective environment. However, Mr. Zhang Fakui launched a compulsory education movement in the 52 counties of the four provincial border areas under his jurisdiction under the circumstances where these difficulties have not decreased.

After Zhang made up his mind, he issued a compulsory education order in the name of the commander-in-chief and designated Jiangshan, the county where he was stationed, as an experimental county, and Chenxiang Town as a pilot area. He set a deadline to eliminate all illiteracy in the entire area. He organized a compulsory education implementation committee and cadres, opened 18 simple literacy schools, and divided more than 1,200 illiterate people in the town into teams and loaded them into these 18 train carriages. The engine turned, the compulsory train started, and it followed the rails on time and achieved the door of success. On the day of the graduation ceremony, the reporter also went to participate. I saw those students from teenagers to forty or fifty years old, most of whom were barefoot and wore straw sandals. The students with the best grades received prizes such as watches and ink boxes, and the rest received at least letter paper and diplomas. Not to mention that they were all happy, even the reporter was extremely happy!

Page 9

Minister Kong Talks About the Financial Situation in Guangdong Province - Expected to Return to Normal Soon - Has Telegraphed Zou, Song, Tang, and Gu to Consider the People's Livelihood and Eliminate Exorbitant Taxes, Miscellaneous Levies, and Illegal Salt Surcharges as Much as Possible - Denies That an Important Military and Political Conference Will Be Held in Lushan 99

Xinxin News Agency reports: Kong Xiangxi, Vice President of the Executive Yuan and Minister of Finance, originally planned to leave Shanghai for Beijing the night before last and then go to Lushan. However, due to the heavy financial burden and the slight damage to the patrol ship he planned to take, he postponed his departure until last night and took the overnight express train to Beijing and then to Lushan. A reporter from Xinxin News Agency paid a visit to Finance Minister Kong at his private residence on Simus Road last night and inquired about everything. Kong received him and said that Song Ziliang, the special commissioner of Guangdong's finance and director of the finance department, had arrived in Guangdong to take office and had sent a telegram to the Ministry of Finance. It is expected that the financial situation in Guangdong Province will soon return to normal after Zou, the vice minister, and Song, the special commissioner, have reorganized it. It is investigated that over the years, Guangdong Province has levied many exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous levies, causing great suffering to the people of Guangdong. Because they are under tyranny, they have no way to appeal. Therefore, I (Kong) have telegraphed Zou and Song, asking them to consider the people's livelihood and eliminate exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous levies that are harmful to society as much as possible. At the same time, I have also telegraphed Tang, the salt transport commissioner (Hai'an), to also eliminate illegal salt surcharges in order to relieve the people's plight. Liu Jiwen, the mayor of Guangzhou, came north a few days ago. I have already met with him. He came because no one could maintain local order in Guangzhou after Chen Jitang left. Therefore, I telegraphed Hong Kong and asked Chairman Lin (Yunhai) and Liu to hurry back to the province. After they arrived in the province, Lin immediately sent him to the north as a representative of the provincial government to report on the local situation. According to him, the people of Guangdong Province feel very grateful for the central government's settlement of the Guangdong incident and its peaceful handling, which did not cause any harm to the people. Therefore, they extremely support the central military and political authorities. Local order is also gradually recovering. However, they hope that Director Yu (Hanmou) will come to Guangzhou as soon as possible so that everything can be presided over. He knows that Yu has arrived in the province after arriving in Shanghai. The people's hearts will become more stable. Regarding the fact that the central military and political officials are going to Lushan this time, it is entirely for the purpose of working in another place. It is common practice for administrative leaders in various countries around the world to work in another place during the hot summer months. The reason is that the weather is hot and everyone's energy is inevitably a little less. Those who bear important responsibilities and have busy duties must find ways to remedy this. Therefore, the climate in the capital is hot, and various countries invariably work in another place. This time, the central colleagues accompanied Chairman Lin and President Jiang to Gu, which is actually an example of international practice. Outsiders who do not understand this say that the central officials are going to Lushan to escape the heat, which is actually a misrepresentation. As for those who do not know the truth and spread rumors that the central government will hold an important military and political conference in Lushan, it is even more absurd. If the central government needs to convene a conference, it can gather anytime, anywhere. Why go to Lushan to create this rumor? If it is not with ulterior motives, it is because they do not understand the truth.

National Products Factory Association; Submitting a List of Restrictions on Tax Exemption Methods 105

In order to prevent smuggling, the National Products Factory Association of this city sent a telegram to the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry yesterday, and submitted seven items of methods to restrict the exchange of cotton yarn tax bills for cotton cloth export tax exemption permits. The details are recorded as follows:

Telegram to the Two Ministries

The association sent a telegram to the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry yesterday, saying, "Presenting a list of methods to restrict the exchange of cotton yarn tax bills for cotton cloth export tax exemption permits, requesting approval and adoption, ordering the Su, Zhejiang, and Anhui Unified Tax Bureau to issue a notice for implementation, in order to prevent smuggling and maintain the national cloth industry. It is the proposal of Zhou Shixuan, representative of the Qin Gong Sheng Ji Dyeing and Weaving Factory at the 10th Joint Meeting of the Executive and Supervisory Committees of the Association, to submit a list of methods to restrict the exchange of cotton yarn tax bills for cotton cloth exports, in order to use tax exemption permits to prevent smuggling. After notifying the relevant factories to submit opinions and referring to the actual situation, seven items of methods were drafted and submitted to the 11th Joint Meeting of the Executive and Supervisory Committees on July 3 for deliberation, requesting the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry to adopt and implement them, etc." The methods to restrict the exchange of cotton yarn tax bills for cotton cloth export permits have been drafted and submitted for approval. It is hoped that your ministry will investigate and verify, and give approval and implementation.

Seven Items of Methods

(1) All cotton spinning and dyeing factories, pure dyeing factories, pure cloth factories, and cloth shops that are capitalized and operated within the Shanghai city area shall re-register in accordance with the registration methods of each factory and cloth shop notified by the Su, Zhejiang, and Anhui Unified Tax Bureau in order to enjoy the benefit of exchanging cotton yarn tax bills for cotton cloth exports and tax exemption permits. All unregistered factories and shops shall not be allowed to exchange cotton yarn tax bills for cotton cloth export tax exemption permits, in order to prevent smuggling. (2) When weaving factories apply for registration, they shall separately indicate the actual number of electric looms and wooden looms, and the number of cloth that each loom can produce per day (for example, if each loom operates day and night, it can produce about four bolts of 30-yard cloth. If the whole factory has 100 looms, it can produce 12,000 bolts of cloth per month. This is based on electric looms. The output of wooden looms is half of that. By analogy, the number should be increased or decreased). According to the actual output of the factory, it shall be allowed to exchange an equal amount of cotton yarn tax bills for cotton cloth export tax exemption permits, in order to facilitate the promotion of national cloth. (3) Pure dyeing factories and cloth shops have no weaving machines at all. The grey cloth used by dyeing factories and the cloth purchased by cloth shops must be purchased from spinning factories or pure weaving factories. The grey cloth or any cloth purchased by the factory or shop shall be registered with the original yarn tax bill and the invoice from the weaving factory to the competent Unified Tax Bureau (the registration form shall be issued by the Unified Tax Bureau). Once the cloth is loaded for export, the original registration form, the shipping mark, and the original yarn tax bill shall be checked for consistency before being allowed to exchange for cotton cloth export tax exemption permits and transported in accordance with the regulations. However, the quantity of cloth sold varies, and it shall be allowed to transport in batches with a single invoice, with the number of bolts noted each time and stamped by the Unified Tax Bureau until the shipment is completed. (4) The Unified Tax Bureau shall prepare an investigation form to investigate and register the names and quantities of existing cloths in pure weaving factories, pure dyeing factories, and cloth shops. If they have already obtained cloth export permits, it shall be verified whether the quantity of cloth prepared for export is consistent. Each factory and shop shall not purchase surplus cotton yarn tax bills on the market to fraudulently exchange for cloth export permits and tax exemption permits. If any fraudulent activities are found, they shall be punished in accordance with the anti-smuggling regulations. (5) The Unified Tax Bureau shall crack down on the fraudulent activities of counterfeit factories. In this city, weaving factories often falsely hang up a signboard of a certain weaving factory, and their purpose is to purchase cloth export tax exemption permits in the market in the name of the weaving factory to smuggle and commit fraud. All such counterfeit factories are responsible. If there are two or more signboards in one factory, the production of Factory A and Factory B shall be investigated. If the weaving machine production is inconsistent with the account book, it shall be deemed as fraudulently obtaining permits, smuggling, and committing fraud, and shall be severely punished as a warning to others. (6) If inland weaving factories have wholesale outlets in Shanghai, they shall present the cotton cloth export tax exemption permits issued by the competent Unified Tax Office to the Shanghai Unified Tax Bureau for verification and stamping before the goods can be transported. (7) Pure weaving factories shall not exchange export tax permits for more than the production quantity of the factory's weaving machines each month. Dyeing factories and cloth shops shall not exceed the cloth registered with the bureau in the registration form, in order to prevent smuggling.

Agricultural Capital Bureau Ready for Establishment; Banks Forming Agricultural Banking Syndicate 106

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, the Ministry of Industry and various banks jointly prepared to establish the Agricultural Capital Bureau with a total of 60 million yuan in fixed and joint funds. After the government allocated funds and the banks jointly determined the amount, the banks formed an agricultural loan banking syndicate. The details are recorded as follows:

Established in August

The Agricultural Capital Bureau is ready for establishment and is scheduled to be established in August. According to Article 14 of the Articles of Association, the Board of Directors shall consist of 23 directors. In addition to the nine directors designated by the Minister of Industry Wu Dingchang, the Minister of Interior Jiang Zuobin, the Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi, the Minister of Railways Yu Feihong, the Secretary-General of the National Economic Commission Qin Fen, the Director of the Agricultural Department of the Ministry of Industry Xu Tinghu, the Director of the Central Agricultural Experiment Institute Xie Jiasheng, and the Director of the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau Cai Wuji, etc., the Ministry of Industry will select two more people, and the remaining twelve will be elected by the banks that undertake the joint funds. Now, the banks have decided to hold a meeting this week to elect them. It is heard that Wu Dingchang will be recommended as the chairman of the board, and Zou Bingwen will be the general manager.

Forming Agricultural Loan Syndicate

A fixed capital of 30 million yuan will be allocated by the government in five years starting from this year. A joint fund of 30 million yuan will be jointly paid by the banks in five years starting from this year. Regarding working capital, according to Article 4 of the Articles of Association, "The agricultural loan syndicate organized by the participating banks shall agree with the Agricultural Capital Bureau on the amount at the beginning of each year." Now, Zou Bingwen, the general manager of the Shanghai Bank, and Qian Xinzhi, the general manager of the Four Banks Savings Association, are responsible for contacting the banks, and have obtained the approval of the banks. The number of working capital and detailed methods are being negotiated. It will be announced after the Agricultural Capital Bureau opens for business.

Dredging and Excavation of the Shentan in the Huangpu River; Recent Project; Limited Time to Complete Preliminary Completion; 800,000 Yuan of Mud and Sand Has Been Excavated 108

According to Datong News Agency, the Huangpu River Dredging Bureau ordered the world's largest dredger, the Jianshe, from Germany. After arriving in Shanghai in April last year, it sailed to Shentan (also known as Tonghe Shansha) outside the Wusongkou to start dredging. This dredging project has been going on for a year. The recent progress of the project is recorded below:

Shentan Dredging

The Jianshe dredger is the world's latest trailing suction type. It can continue to operate while dredging without anchoring, so its work efficiency is extremely high. The amount of soil recently dredged from the dredging area is about 80 million cubic meters (4 tons per cubic meter). The work is still limited to daytime. Plans are now being made to add night shifts. However, the dredging area is on the proper waterway, and there is frequent traffic of ships, so it is quite difficult.

Adding New Ships

The bureau plans to complete the preliminary dredging of Shentan in five years. The dredgers are set at two, so the construction of the second one began on March 18 this year. However, in order to take into account the round-trip time for bids from foreign shipping companies, there must be sufficient time, so it has not yet been determined which country's shipping company will undertake the construction. The dredger will still be of the trailing suction type, but the hull will be larger than the Jianshe. It is expected to be completed in a year and a half.

Construction Model

The Jianshe dredger of the bureau was ordered from the German Schichau Shipyard and represented by the Siemens Foreign Company in this port. Before the ship was completed, Schichau Company first built a model of the ship, which was very exquisite, and handed it over to Siemens Foreign Company for display. Now that the Jianshe ship has been working for more than a year and the use is satisfactory, the acceptance procedures have been officially completed, so the ship model has been sent by Siemens Foreign Company to the Huangpu River Dredging Bureau for display.

Leather Goods Sent to the United States Must Include Name, Address, Number, and Type 109

The U.S. Consul General's Office in Shanghai recently received a telegram from the United States stating that all leather goods shipped from China to various parts of the United States, whether shipped by mail or by other means, or originally shipped to one port and then transshipped to another port in the United States, must henceforth clearly write the name and address of the shipper and the consignee, and the number and type of all items in the package on the outside of the package in accordance with the regulations passed by the 74th Congress.

This Year's Tea Export Volume Has Increased Sharply; The Value Increased by 30,000 Metric Tons in June Alone Compared to Last Year; European Merchants Observe That There Is Hope for the Revival of Chinese Tea 110

According to Xin Xin News Agency, this year's tea trade with foreign countries has undergone major reforms in quality and sales, and the selling price has doubled, and exports are strong, and the situation is quite auspicious for the revival. The details are recorded as follows:

Doubled in the Past

According to a report from the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, in June, Shanghai's tea exports were 39,607.13 metric tons of green tea, 12,908.77 metric tons of black tea, and 1,880.47 metric tons of other tea, totaling 54,396.37 metric tons, an increase of about 30,000 metric tons compared to the same month last year, and an increase of more than 49,000 metric tons compared to May of this year. The purchasers were the United States, France, Britain, Germany, the Netherlands, Morocco, and other countries. Green tea accounted for the largest share of exports, and black tea accounted for only two-fifths of green tea, because the demand for black tea is not as widespread as that for green tea.

The Market Is Still Thriving

This year, tea exports have increased, and the selling price is better than last year. Since the market opened, the market price of various high-end box teas, except for inferior goods, has been between 60 and 70 yuan. This month, tea merchants from Britain, France, Russia, and the United States in Shanghai still have a great need for it, such as Pingshui Xiushui and Shrimp Eyes, with thousands of boxes traded every day, especially Pingshui green tea, which sells the best. Although the arrival of goods is eagerly awaited, there is still a situation of supply falling short of demand, so the foreign sales situation is still very prosperous.

Reasons for Improvement

As for the reasons for the sudden improvement in foreign sales, according to what the reporter of Xin Xin News Agency learned from inquiries, it can be divided into three points: (1) Since China has been developing tea on its own, in addition to implementing centralized sales, the National Economic Council and tea merchants in Anhui and Jiangxi have jointly run experimental fields to promote scientific roasting methods, and the quality has been improved day by day, surpassing Indian and Ceylon tea; (2) Although Britain, Russia, the United States, France, and other countries have advocated tea planting, it is difficult to achieve results due to unsuitable land; (3) The production of tea in India, Java, Ceylon, and other countries that compete with Chinese tea in the international market has decreased sharply in recent years, and Chinese tea has taken advantage of the shortage, so European tea merchants in general observe that if Chinese tea can work hard to reform and not slack off, it can be expected to dominate the international tea market in a few years.

Preparations for the National Products Year Conference in the City; Yangtze River Inspection Group 116

The City National Products Year Movement Committee, recognizing that the Yangtze River basin was originally a wealthy area of our country, but has suffered frequent disasters in recent years and been affected by the dumping of foreign goods, leading to economic decline and hardship for the people in the provinces along the river, plans to unite several Shanghai industrial and financial magnates and well-known national product manufacturers to form a Yangtze River inspection group. This is aimed at understanding the situation of foreign goods dumping and exploring ways to lend funds to the inland, so as to lay the groundwork for future overall planning of national product production and sales, and inland investment. Preparations are now underway. The outline of the Yangtze River inspection group formulated by the committee is as follows: (1) The group is named the Shanghai City National Products Year Yangtze River Inspection Group. (2) The purpose of the group is to investigate the economic conditions of the provinces along the Yangtze River, so as to comprehensively plan the production and sales of national products and the way for investment and lending. (3) The group is jointly organized by Shanghai industrialists, financiers, and national product manufacturers. (4) The inspection route of the group starts from Shanghai, along the various ports of the Yangtze River, to Chengdu, Sichuan. (5) The scope of the group’s inspection includes: A. Industrial situation; B. Commercial situation; C. Rural economy; D. Local tax system; E. Organization of industrial and commercial groups; F. Investigation of national product raw materials and famous local products; G. Other matters related to industry and finance. (6) The inspection period of the group is two months. (7) The number of members of the group is limited to thirty, and one president and one vice president are publicly elected to preside over the national inspection affairs. (8) When necessary, the group may be divided into groups for inspection by the president's temporary decision. (9) The expenses required by the group shall be borne by the participating members themselves. (10) The preparation office of the group is located at the City National Products Year Movement Committee of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce at Tianhou Palace Bridge.

Shanghai-Wuxi Automobile Company; Reducing Gasoline Consumption; Achievements of Retrofitting Charcoal Furnaces 119

According to the Central News Agency, the Shanghai-Wuxi Long-Distance Automobile Company has been open to traffic for almost a year since August 15 last year. Yesterday, the reporter met Mr. Jiang Yuren, the director of the general affairs department of the company, to inquire about the recent situation of the company. According to his talk, the company's business situation in the past year is currently being counted, and it is generally quite good. The company's only plan at present is to reduce the consumption of gasoline in order to increase net profit. The important step of this plan is to adopt charcoal and diesel vehicles. The company had previously decided to retrofit all vehicles with charcoal-for-oil furnaces by Zhongming Factory. Twenty-eight vehicles have now been installed, and the test results in the past six months are very good, no different from those using gasoline, and the consumption is saved a lot. However, due to the insufficient availability of vehicles, the installation can only be carried out gradually. In addition, the company has eight diesel vehicles, which were originally purchased for freight transportation. Because there is still little freight transportation at present, they have been converted into passenger cars, and the oil consumption is also quite economical. However, the cost of the car body is huge and more will be placed. At present, the company's daily vehicles give priority to charcoal cars, followed by diesel cars, and the use of gasoline cars is decreasing day by day, and detailed numerical comparisons of these three different fuels are being made, which will be completed soon to contribute to the reference for adoption by various highways.

Songjiang Salt Production Workers' Union; Letter to Ningbo Fellow Villagers Association; Yuanpu Salt Field Limited Quota for Salt Payment; Please Forward to Revoke the Order 120

The Ningbo Fellow Villagers Association received a letter from the Songjiang County Salt Production Industry Union yesterday, saying: Sir, according to reports from hundreds of members of our association, such as Wang Dingxiang, Mao Zhongfu, and Zhang Xiaohuai, because they recently saw Notice No. 69 issued by the Yuanpu Salt Field Office, it stated: "According to Order No. 6345 of June 1 of this year from the Songjiang Salt Affairs Audit Sub-Office, after translation, it is found that the salt production by the board households in the Songjiang District is based on the voluntary application of the board households for a special permit for salt production and drying, without any coercion from the public. The board households voluntarily and conscientiously abide by the salt production regulations and pay at least 317.5 market catties of salt per board every year as stipulated by the Salt Affairs Department. If the salt paid is less than the fixed quota by the end of this year, a fine shall be imposed (the shortage of salt money shall be paid at the price of 2.7 cents per dan of salt in the storehouse), or their special permit shall be revoked, the salt board shall be broken, and no excuses of poverty shall be used to hope for exemption from the fine. In addition, the households that have not paid granules from January to April this year shall be strictly ordered to find a corresponding guarantee, and the salt shall be paid in full thereafter, otherwise their special permit shall be revoked, the salt board shall be broken, and no leniency shall be given. We should comply with this order, etc." Upon receiving this order, the salt farmers in the entire field were in an uproar and panic. It is necessary to know that the leniency and severity of legislation must be adapted to human feelings. The salt production situation in the Songjiang Field is not fully understood by the superiors. Now we will carefully present it as follows: (omitted) Such notices that are out of reason and emotion, the salt farmers absolutely dare not obey, and request to forward to the superiors to revoke the order, and must not deceive and conceal, and weep and plead, and wait quietly for a clear order, etc. Based on this, after our association verified that the statements made by the members are all true, it is the key point of salt production, which depends entirely on sunlight, tides, and manpower. Although the payment quota has been stipulated, the output is still difficult to predict. The salt production is produced by nature, and cannot be manufactured by machines, so it can be expedited. The life of the salt farmers is unspeakably bitter, and it is difficult to make ends meet all year round. We hope that the weather will be clear for a long time in the second half of the year, and the tides will be greater, so that the previous losses can be made up. If the weather is bad again, not only will it be difficult to pay the quota, but the livelihood of the salt farmers will be impossible to solve. Where will this fine come from? If they must revoke the permit and break the salt board to cut off the livelihood of the salt farmers, the salt farmers are at the critical moment of life and death. Indeed, I am afraid that an incident will be caused. Our association advises the salt farmers to pay as much as they can. We also found that there are many members of your association who rely on salt production for a living in Songjiang. In addition to presenting to the salt administration authorities, we have specially written to your association to uphold justice, hoping that you will forward it to the Songjiang Salt Transport Deputy Envoy to order the Yuanpu Salt Field to revoke the order to relieve the salt farmers' suffering and maintain their livelihood. This is a true public friendship."

This association wants to complete its mission as soon as possible, and has sent personnel to assist in handling it separately. Other organizations such as the Chamber of Commerce, Education Association, Federation of Trade Unions, and Bankers Association are also working hard to promote it. As for entertainment venues, this association has sent letters requesting a fixed day to use the business income to make donations. Various theaters, movie theaters, amusement parks, and dance halls have held activities one after another, and the results are still good. Venues that have not yet held activities are in contact and will be held on a fixed date, so that they can be concluded as soon as possible. In addition, the collection of aviation salvation funds from the cooked water industry was originally decided to be piloted for one month from August 1. Due to various reasons, it has been notified to temporarily stop, so as to avoid disputes. The collection situation of the hotel industry, fresh meat industry, and civil ship industry is very good, etc. Then, after each field director reported the progress of the inspection and contact, they discussed the fundraising policy and other cases until the meeting adjourned at 4:30.

Rice and Wheat Improvement Institute; Testing Rice Varieties; Plans to Implement the Plan; Submitted to the Ministry for Trial Implementation 123

According to the Industrial News Agency, the National Rice and Wheat Improvement Institute believes that the improvement of rice and wheat should start with the improvement of varieties. At the beginning of its establishment, the institute engaged in breeding work and made preliminary promotion in suitable areas, in order to actively improve quality and increase yield. However, my country has a vast territory, and the rice-producing areas are vast. The local conditions vary greatly. The original improved varieties cannot meet the general needs of various regions, and there is no shortage of excellent varieties in various regions that can be selected. However, it is a pity that farmers have shallow knowledge and do not know how to choose and plant superior varieties. In order to eliminate inferior varieties in various places, guide farmers to select good varieties, and improve rice yield and quality, it is planned to conduct pilot tests in the important rice-producing areas of Jiangsu, Jiangxi, Hunan, and Anhui provinces first, to test local small rice varieties, in order to establish a center for superior rice varieties, and gradually promote them to other areas. A general outline of the implementation plan for the 25th year of pilot rice variety testing and a brief chapter on the Rice Variety Testing Committee of each county are submitted to the Ministry of Industry, and the governments of Jiangsu, Jiangxi, Hunan, and Anhui provinces are divided to order the counties to conduct them in accordance with the pilot chapters.

Washing Vegetables on the Side of the Boat; Girl Drowned to Death in the Luhun River 130

A local, Xu Jintao, lived by shaking a dung boat. At about 6:00 pm yesterday, he docked the boat at the Jiangyuan Lane Pier on the Suzhou River. At that time, Xu's 13-year-old daughter, San Meizi, squatted down to wash vegetables on the side of the boat. Accidentally, she fell into the water and immediately sank and drowned. By the time she was salvaged, she could not be recovered. Xu Jintao, a member of the corpse family, arrived at the scene and confirmed that the deceased was indeed his daughter, San Meizi, and immediately issued a certificate to receive and collect the corpse.
